***горделивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горделивый.html>гордели́вый</a> (11943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Presumably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">гърдѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gŭrděti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be proud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">гордѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorděti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гордый.html>го́рдый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górdyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гордиться.html>горди́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gordítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***гордый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гордый.html>го́рдый</a> (3439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gъrdъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гордый.html>го́рдый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górdyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гордый.html>го́рдый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>proud</li>
<li>majestic</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>горе</a> (1554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>го́ре</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">góre</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>го́ря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>го́ря</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горе.html>горь</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>горе́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">goré</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> up

***горелка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лка</a> (28168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>burner (of a gas range, heater or light using liquid or gas fuel).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лка</a></b> бу́нзена</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gorélka</b> Búnzena</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Bunsen <b>burner</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The nozzle of a welding torch.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">горі́лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">horílka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">горі́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">horíty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Similar to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">гарэ́лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">harélka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Russia" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Russia">Southern Russia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vodka, usually in a Ukrainian context.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1835</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikolai_Gogol" class="extiw" title="w:Nikolai Gogol">Nikolai Gogol</a>,  <cite>Тарас <a href = vnd.unilang:бульб.html>Бу́льба</a></cite>  | <cite>=<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Taras_Bulba" class="extiw" title="w:Taras Bulba">Taras Bulʹba</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">... <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b> побо́льше, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдумка.html>вы́думками</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изюм.html>изю́мом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кими</a> вытребеньками, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенный.html>пе́нной</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:горелка.html>горе́лки</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шипеть.html>шипе́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бешеный.html>бе́шеная</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">... da <b>gorélki</b> pobólʹše, ne s výdumkami <b>gorélki</b>, ne s izjúmom i vsjákimi vytrebenʹkami, a čístoj pennoj <b>gorélki</b>, štob igrála i šipéla, kak béšenaja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">... and more <b>gorelka</b>, not with fantasies of <b>gorelka</b>, not with raisins and all kinds of frippery, but clean foaming <b>gorelka</b>, to sparkle and hiss like crazy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Used in place of the synonym <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vódka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> to allude to Ukrainian village custom.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>горе́</a>(ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">goré(tʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горелый.html>горе́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorélyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>burnt</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́л</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ла</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ло</a>, *горе́лы</span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to past-tense forms of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare e.g. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorélo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it burned</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).</li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горемыка.html>горемы́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">goremýka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горемыка.html>горемы́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горемыка.html>горемы́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горемыка.html>горемы́к</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горение.html>горе́ние</a> (21263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горение.html>горе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горение.html>горе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горение.html>горе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горение.html>горе́ний</a></b>)

***гореть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a> (874)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gorěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгореть.html>сгоре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svečá <b>goréla</b> na stolé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A candle <b>was burning</b> on the table.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be alight</li>
<li>to gleam, to shine (of eyes)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгорать.html>сгора́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sgorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***горизонт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нт</a> (2318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὁρίζων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">horízōn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorizónt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нтов</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонталь.html>горизонта́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorizontálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонталь.html>горизонта́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонталь.html>горизонта́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонталь.html>горизонта́лей</a></b>)

***горисполком.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горисполком.html>горисполком</a> (22481)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городской.html>городско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполком.html>исполко́м</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorodskój ispolkóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in turn acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городской.html>городско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorodskój ispolnítelʹnyj komitét</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">city executive committee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горисполком.html>горисполко́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorispolkóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горисполком.html>горисполко́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горисполком.html>горисполко́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горисполком.html>горисполко́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Soviet Union</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> city executive committee</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горланить.html>горла́нить</a> (22721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górlo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">throat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + an unclear suffix + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***горло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a> (1362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">гърло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gŭrlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gъrdlo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>throat</li>
<li>gullet</li>
<li>neck (of a vessel)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горловой.html>горлово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gorlovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> throat

<li>guttural, deep-throat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горловой.html>горлово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gorlovój</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>guttural</b> voice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горловой.html>горлово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пение.html>пе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gorlovóje</b> pénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>guttural/deep-throat</b> singing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горница.html>го́рница</a> (7887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">горьнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorĭnĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>гора́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain, heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горница.html>го́рница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горница.html>го́рницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горница.html>го́рницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горница.html>го́рниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> room, chamber; cenacle; ben, ben-room</li></ol>

***горный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a> (2661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>гора́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">górnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mountain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>górnaja</b> dolína</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mountain</b> valley</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хруста́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>górnyj</b> xrustálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>rock</b> crystal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mining
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инженер.html>инжене́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>górnyj</b> inženér</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mining</b> engineer</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геологический.html>геологи́ческий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">geologíčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">горнодобыва́ющий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gornodobyvájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
